[30;1m27 | [0m[35mTwo environment variables can be used to control the logging:[0m
[30;1m28 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m30 | [0m[35m      ibmq-provider modules. If an invalid level is set, the log level defaults to ``WARNING``.[0m
